create table Customer
(
    email        varchar(320)  not null
        primary key,
    password     char(60)      not null,
    fullname     varchar(200)  null,
    address      varchar(200)  null,
    phone        char(11)      null,
    gender       varchar(20)   null,
    status       int           not null,
    profileImage varchar(2000) null,
    dob          bigint        null,
    deviceID     varchar(1000) null
);
